# ED Orientation

**Status.** Living single-file orientation reference for the Event Density (ED) framework. Updated in place as the program evolves — no version freezing, no v1.x file chain. Last substantive update: 2026-04-23 (seventeenth pass — F4 Correlation-class sub-arc **CLOSED** via nine-memo arc: canonical Inconclusive (pair sparsity); F4-alt Inconclusive strict / Refuted-by-extension structural (C(r) saturated at ~2 from r=1.0 lu); F4-alt-refine Inconclusive-thin (lattice-discretisation obstruction: Δr < 0.41 lu under-resolves square-Z² inter-site distances); F4 Integration memo synthesises three-line verdict).

**Citation form.** Cite by section, not by version. Example: "ED-Orientation §6.9" for the ED-SC 2.0 invariance statement. If a point-in-time snapshot is ever needed for an external paper citation, use git's commit SHA of this file rather than a version number in the filename.

**How to use.** Read §1 first (scope + discrepancy map with repo). §3.1 disambiguates the two P1–P7 axiom sets (derivation vs. Canon). §5.9 is the meta-claim (laws / symmetries as emergent). §6.9 is the current canonical cross-scale invariance statement (ED-SC 2.0). **§7 is the five-test empirical-status table** with links to all five operational protocols (AFM / UDM-FRAP / ED-09.5 Track A / ED-09.5 Track B / C7 Triad-Coupling). **The Test-to-Axiom Mapping Report at [`docs/ED-Test-to-Axiom-Mapping-v1.0.md`](ED-Test-to-Axiom-Mapping-v1.0.md)** is the 18×5 coverage matrix that drove the C7 addition. §11 is the Emergence-Universe sandbox (pre-ED proof-of-concept). §2 for the paper trajectory. §8 for full inventory (Desktop + PhilArchive + GitHub). §9 for question-type routing.

**Recent substantive updates (in descending chronological order — move each up when you supersede it, delete items once they're fully absorbed into the body text):**

It is a *re-reading* that supplies ontological grounding for results already correctly placed. No closed arc re-opens. - **2026-04-24 (QM-EMERGENCE ARC CLOSED — structurally complete).** Five-step QM-emergence derivation + tightening program completed in this session. Non-relativistic single-particle QM's four independent postulates (state, evolution, measurement, observables) reduced to structural consequences of the participation measure `P_K = √(b_K) · e^{iπ_K}` + four-band bandwidth decomposition + commitment dynamics, with minimal empirical anchoring of ℏ and m. **Executed work:** (a) Step 1 [`quantum/foundations/participation_measure.md`](../quantum/foundations/participation_measure.md) — provisional definition of the participation measure; nine structural constraints C1–C9; fusion of Primitive 04 bandwidth + Primitive 09 polarity phase into a single complex-valued object. (b) Step 2 [`quantum/foundations/schrodinger_emergence.md`](../quantum/foundations/schrodinger_emergence.md) — derivation of the linear Schrödinger equation `iℏ ∂_t Ψ = Ĥ Ψ` as the thin-participation limit (M_eff → ∞, environmental band suppressed) of the coherent-sum `Ψ = Σ_K P_K`; Madelung transformation giving continuity + Hamilton-Jacobi-with-quantum-pressure. (c) Step 3 [`quantum/foundations/born_rule_from_participation.md`](../quantum/foundations/born_rule_from_participation.md) — Born rule `Prob(K*) = |P_K*|² / Σ|P_K|²` derived as FORCED consequence of environmental phase-randomization + individuation threshold + definitional `b_K = |P_K|²`. Squared-amplitude form is DEFINITIONAL, not postulated. (d) Step 4 [`quantum/foundations/bell_correlations_from_participation.md`](../quantum/foundations/bell_correlations_from_participation.md) — Bell-CHSH violations up to Tsirelson bound 2√2 from non-factorizable joint participation P^{AB}. LHV bound `|S| ≤ 2` for factorizable; 2√2 at singlet Tsirelson angles derived via Landau-Khalfin operator-norm algebra. No-signaling FORCED by commitment locality. (e) Step 5 [`quantum/foundations/uncertainty_from_participation.md`](../quantum/foundations/uncertainty_from_participation.md) — Heisenberg Δx · Δp ≥ ℏ/2 from Fourier-conjugate partition `b^{adj} = b_x + b_p` of the adjacency bandwidth + Fourier-uncertainty theorem applied to Ψ. Same derivation generalizes to ΔE·Δt, ΔN·Δφ, spin. (f) Synthesis [`quantum/foundations/qm_emergence_synthesis.md`](../quantum/foundations/qm_emergence_synthesis.md) — archival integration of Steps 1–5; identifies the exponent-2 thread (same 2 in Born `|P|²`, Schrödinger kinetic `ℏ²k²/(2m)`, Madelung `√ρ`, sublinear composition, Heisenberg `(Δx·Δp)²`) as the program's strongest positive claim. None is a structural gap in the QM-emergence chain. **Guardrails:** (a) the arc is closed structurally; do not reopen unless new primitive-level derivation path is identified. - **2026-04-24 (second-half session — distinguishing-signature archive resolution + temporal-platform scaffolding + SESSION STOPPING POINT).** After the first-half 13-primitive stack + Q-C retrodiction pipeline was built and OAM'd, the second-half session pursued the distinguishing-signature path and produced four additional memos resolving Problem 2 of `distinguishing_signatures.md` and building temporal-platform scaffolds. **Executed work:** (a) [`quantum/effective_theory/signature_observable_mapping.md`](../quantum/effective_theory/signature_observable_mapping.md) — archive read of ED-Phys-16 + ED-Phys-17 RESOLVED Problem 2. **N_osc ≈ 9 is TEMPORAL** (ED-Phys-17 §4.1 peak-height oscillation count 8 baseline, 10–19 on backgrounds). **Q ≈ 3.5 is TEMPORAL** (damped-oscillator quality factor). **Triad coupling ≈ 0.03 is MIXED** (ED-Phys-16 §12.3: `A_generated/A_parent² = 0.76/5² = 0.030`). **Discrepancy flagged: Q-C Boundary paper says "3rd harmonic at 3–6%" but ED-Phys-16 §7.2, §9, §12.1 clearly reports 2nd harmonic at 3–6%.** Wording error in the Q-C Boundary paper; amplitude correct, harmonic order wrong. **Corrected testability map:** N_osc and Q require temporal-platform data (cavity QED / SC qubits / optomechanics / BEC); triad coupling and 2nd harmonic are mixed/spatial but require detector-plane projection derivations not yet done. Matter-wave fringe data (Eibenberger, Fein) cannot test N_osc or Q. (c) [`quantum/effective_theory/sc_qubit_pde_mapping.md`](../quantum/effective_theory/sc_qubit_pde_mapping.md) — Phase 0 derivation attempted. **Structural mismatch discovered: canonical ED PDE is spatial (∇²) while a qubit is 0-dimensional.** Under 0-D reduction (Option A), the mobility channel `M(ρ)∇²ρ` drops out entirely — only penalty + participation channels remain. (d) [`quantum/retrodictions/optomechanics_scaffold.md`](../quantum/retrodictions/optomechanics_scaffold.md) — optomech ring-down and BEC collective-mode decay scaffold. **Spatial-relaxation structure preserved** (mechanical modes have spatial profiles; BEC collective modes are intrinsically spatial). (ii) **The canonical ED PDE is spatial; 0-D systems (qubits) lose the mobility channel under reduction.** ED-Phys-17's N_osc prediction was derived for spatially-extended peak relaxation into a surrounding medium and may not transfer cleanly to 0-D observables. (iii) **Platform-bridge derivations are the core Phase-2 program.** Four Phase-0-analog attempts this session (matter-wave, SC qubit, optomech/BEC — plus envelope-correction factor-12 discrepancy) all surfaced structural issues specific to platform-bridge derivations. The ED primitive stack is internally consistent; the ED PDE layer is internally consistent; the cross-level bridges are systematically under-developed. Each platform (matter-wave, SC qubit, optomechanics, BEC, cavity QED, cosmological) needs a dedicated `*_pde_mapping.md` memo giving ε_k / ζ / τ / D_E / ρ / v identifications uniquely. (iv) **Recommended first executable temporal retrodiction: Jin et al. 1997 BEC collective-mode data** once the Phase-0 ε_k / ζ derivation for BEC is completed. **SESSION STOPPING POINT.** Four sequential Phase-0-analog derivations hit structural blockers; program state is cleaner than at session start but further progress requires dedicated platform-bridge derivations. (d) [`theory/ED_SC_3_4_twopoint_FilterRelaxation_Driver.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_4_twopoint_FilterRelaxation_Driver.md) + [`analysis/scripts/ed_sc_3_4_twopoint_correlation_relaxed.py`](../analysis/scripts/ed_sc_3_4_twopoint_correlation_relaxed.py) — F4-alt driver. Execution 2026-04-23: **primary success criterion PASSED** (8 of 10 bins admissible; 27,210 motifs total; 24,464 binned pairs — 480× canonical). **But `C_ensemble(r) ∈ [1.96, 2.05]` across all admissible bins** from r = 1.0 to r = 5.0 lu — saturated at the uncorrelated asymptote `C(∞) = 2`; no C(r) = 1 crossing. Strict verdict Inconclusive; structural reading **Refuted-by-extension** because the half-rise (if any) must lie below r = 1.0 lu, giving ratio < 0.57 — far outside the tenth-pass 0.80 ± 0.05 band. Pearson and Spearman estimators agree to 0.5–2 % (no non-linear rank structure). (e) [`theory/ED_SC_3_4_twopoint_FilterRelaxation_Refine.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_4_twopoint_FilterRelaxation_Refine.md) — F4-alt-refine scope amendment. Δr = 0.25 grid `{0.25, 0.50, 0.75, 1.00, 1.25, 1.50, 1.75, 2.00}` in small-r region to resolve the strict-vs-structural verdict gap. Six-way refined taxonomy: Case A (crossing found → F4 four-way applies) / Case B (no crossing, C ≥ 2 → Refuted) / Case C (no crossing, C < 2 somewhere → Inconclusive-nonmonotone) + `Inconclusive-thin` primary-gate failure. **Durable seventeenth-pass findings (must remain stable across future sessions):** (i) **Canonical F4 cannot measure C(r) at the canonical operating point** — ~2 motifs/snap is too sparse; 94.7 % of pairs land at r > 5.25 lu. This is a structural finding about the filter, not a driver bug. (ii) **F4-alt relaxed filter reveals the motif-filter correlation length is very short** — C(r) already at its uncorrelated asymptote at r = 1.0 lu. The tenth-pass GR-SC 1.7 half-rise compression prediction `r_½^{filt}/r_½^{unfilt} = 0.80 ± 0.05` does not appear supported at the F4-alt operating point; the half-rise (if it exists) lies below r = 1.0 lu (ratio < 0.57, outside [0.70, 0.90]). (iii) **F4-alt-refine EXECUTED 2026-04-23** — [`analysis/scripts/ed_sc_3_4_twopoint_correlation_relaxed_refine.py`](../analysis/scripts/ed_sc_3_4_twopoint_correlation_relaxed_refine.py), artefact `outputs/ed_sc_3_4_twopoint_relaxed_refine/correlation_twopoint_summary.json`. **Verdict Inconclusive-thin** (primary admissibility gate 3/8 < 6 required). Root cause is a **lattice-discretisation obstruction**: on a square integer lattice Z² with minimum-image distance, consecutive achievable radii {1, √2, 2, √5, …} have gaps ≥ √2 − 1 ≈ 0.414 lu, so Δr = 0.25 leaves 5 of 8 bins empty *by construction* regardless of motif count. The three admissible bins (r = 1.0, √2 ≈ 1.414, 2.0) all yield C ∈ [2.04, 2.08] — reinforcing the F4-alt structural Refuted-by-extension reading on the admissible subset. **New lattice-geometry guardrail**: Δr ≥ 0.5 lu is the minimum admissible bin-width on 64² square-Z²; finer r-resolution requires a different ambient geometry, a direct ξ_φ(r) FFT estimator, or a larger lattice rescaled so Δr/ξ ≥ √2 − 1. **F4 sub-arc now CLOSED** by the integration memo [`theory/ED_SC_3_4_twopoint_FilterRelaxation_Integration.md`](../theory/ED_SC_3_4_twopoint_FilterRelaxation_Integration.md) with three-line verdict (§6): (1) canonical (N_req=4): Inconclusive — untested pending larger lattice; (2) relaxed filter (N_req=2): Refuted-by-extension structural — no half-rise in r ≥ 1 lu; (3) scope restriction: F4-alt/F4-alt-refine refutation applies to the C_redshift channel only, canonical operating point and ED-SC distributional invariant untouched. (iv) **Scope restriction holds:** F4-alt and F4-alt-refine are C_redshift(r) measurement only; the canonical `(α_filt=0.25, N_req=4)` operating point remains authoritative for all other ED-SC / GR-SC claims (κ prediction, r*, ℛ_W, C², det G, rigid identities). **Remaining open items post-sub-arc closure:** L-larger follow-up (re-run F4 canonical at N_req=4 on 128²/256² with paired ξ rescaling to unlock the canonical-filter row of GR-SC 1.0 §5 table); direct FFT-based ξ_φ(r) estimator as a parallel measurement channel independent of motif-pair binning; empirical tracks (FRAP at Creative Proteomics, ED-09.5 Aspelmeyer/Arndt outreach — both blocked on external parties); GR-SC 2.1 full revision of 2.0 (tenth-pass open thread, partially addressed by sixteenth-pass Amendment). **Durable memory:** [`memory/project_ed_gr_sc_arc.md`](../../.claude/projects/C--Users-allen-GitHub-Event-Density/memory/project_ed_gr_sc_arc.md) gains a "Seventeenth-pass F4 sub-arc" section with seven-memo enumeration + four durable findings + updated Open threads.

- **2026-04-23 (tenth pass). GR-SC arc opened and consolidated — eight memos, five-class invariant taxonomy for curvature on the kinematic ED acoustic metric.** Following the ninth-pass r* closure, a structural expansion arc examines standard GR curvature invariants on `g_eff = diag(−N²(x), 1, 1)` with `N = √M(ρ_0)` under the same GRF linearisation + canonical ray-endpoint filter used in ED-SC 2.0. **Strictly kinematic**: no Einstein equations, no ADM, no Hawking quantisation (respects `project_ed10_geometry_qft_scope` guardrails). **Eight memos:** [`theory/GR_SC_1_0_EinsteinTensor_MotifStatistics.md`](../theory/GR_SC_1_0_EinsteinTensor_MotifStatistics.md), [`_1_1_Raychaudhuri_`](../theory/GR_SC_1_1_Raychaudhuri_MotifStatistics.md), [`_1_4_AnalogueNEC_MobilityProfiles`](../theory/GR_SC_1_4_AnalogueNEC_MobilityProfiles.md), [`_1_5_HorizonKappa_`](../theory/GR_SC_1_5_HorizonKappa_MotifStatistics.md), [`_1_6_WeylTensor_`](../theory/GR_SC_1_6_WeylTensor_MotifStatistics.md), [`_1_7_Redshift_`](../theory/GR_SC_1_7_Redshift_MotifStatistics.md), [`_1_8_EIT_Extremal_ErrorBudget`](../theory/GR_SC_1_8_EIT_Extremal_ErrorBudget.md), [`_2_0_Consolidation`](../theory/GR_SC_2_0_Consolidation.md). **Durable structural findings (must remain stable across future sessions):** (a) **Five-class invariant taxonomy** — every curvature scalar on `g_eff[ρ_0]` linear in `φ` falls into one of: **Ratio-class** (mobility-universal, typically unbounded): `r*`, `ℛ_Ray = λ_1/λ_2 = r*`, `ℛ_G^{spatial} = r*`, `ℛ_W = −(2r*+1)/(r*+2) ∈ (−2,−1/2)` bounded subclass; **Trace/Gaussian-class** (Gaussian, zero median, scales `|μ₁|σ_2`): `F̄`, `tr(G^{ij})`, scalar `R`; **Quadratic-class** (sign-definite, scales `μ₁²σ_2²`): `C²` (Weyl square), `det(G^{ij})`; **Rayleigh-class** (support `[0,∞)`, scales `|N̂'|σ_1`): `κ` (surface gravity); **Correlation-class** (two-point, scales `μ₁²σ_0²`, depends on `ξ_φ(r)`): `C_redshift(r) = 2[1 − ξ_φ(r)/σ_0²]`. The arc now covers the full `(σ_0, σ_1, σ_2)` spectral triad. (b) **Two rigid identities** — `G_00 ≡ 0` on any static ultrastatic acoustic metric; `B_{ab} ≡ 0` (magnetic Weyl vanishes; all Weyl content is electric). (c) **Mobility-law NEC diagnostic** — `NEC ⟺ (√M)''(ρ) ≥ 0`, equivalently `Q(ρ) = M'' − (M')²/(2M) ≥ 0`. **Canonical ED linear mobility `M = 1−ρ` is NEC-violating** on steep-gradient regions (Q < 0); `(1−ρ)^β` with β ≥ 2, saturating `M_0/(1+αρ)`, and exponential `M_0e^{−αρ}` are NEC-safe. Focusing of null congruences is not universal under default ED mobility; it is locally restored at motif extrema. (d) **Pooled R2 predictions.** Ratio-class: `r* = ℛ_Ray = ℛ_G = −1.88 ± 0.40`, `ℛ_W = −1.23 ± 0.05` (bounded, ×8 sharper). Trace-class: medians rigidly zero. Quadratic-class: `⟨C²⟩ ≈ 2.44·μ₁²σ_2²`, `median(C²) ≈ 2.13·μ₁²σ_2²`, `median(det G) ≈ −0.42·μ₁²σ_2²/N̂²`. Rayleigh-class: `κ_pooled/(|μ₁|σ_1) = 0.52 ± 0.05`. Correlation-class: `C_redshift(0) = 0` and `C_redshift(∞) = 2` rigid; half-rise compression `r_½^{filt}/r_½^{unfilt} = 0.80 ± 0.05` (mobility- and σ_0-universal — cleanest falsifier). (e) **EIT-Extremal error budget integrated (1.8).** The `κ_E/κ_M < 0.1` protocol picks up GRF-induced ratio width `≈ 0.83·σ_κ^{tot}/κ_M^{det}`, with comparable contributions from **intrinsic Rayleigh** (Channel A, σ_1) and **redshift reconstruction noise** (Channel B, σ_0/ℓ_R2); in R2 canonical Channel B ×1.4 dominates. **Engineering falsification-clearance target:** `σ₁/κ_M^{det} < 0.036` (2σ). Deterministic P4-extremal horizons (`κ = 0` at interior maxima) are measure-zero under GRF roughening — generic horizons are non-extremal; direct analogue of how single-seed `r* = −1.304` became pooled `−1.88 ± 0.4`. **Durable memory:** [`memory/project_ed_gr_sc_arc.md`](../../.claude/projects/C--Users-allen-GitHub-Event-Density/memory/project_ed_gr_sc_arc.md) records the eight memos + five-class taxonomy + six guardrails + pooled-R2 prediction block for future sessions. **Guardrails:** (i) all GR-SC claims are (ii)-grade kinematic — do not re-open Einstein/Schwarzschild/α scope; (ii) ratio-class medians are mobility-universal, trace-class medians are rigidly zero, quadratic/Rayleigh/correlation-class predictions must carry explicit (μ₁, σ_0, σ_1, σ_2) context; (iii) the `κ_E/κ_M < 0.1` central prediction is shared with standard analogue gravity — ED's contribution is the calibrated noise model and clearance criterion, not the central value; (iv) NEC diagnostic `Q(ρ)` must be checked before importing any focusing-theorem intuition; (v) `r*` and `ℛ_W` satisfy the algebraic map `ℛ_W = −(2r*+1)/(r*+2)` — these are not independent observables in the clean-saddle limit. **Tangential theoretical targets (not yet executed):** GR-SC 1.2 Geodesics / ED update flows; GR-SC 1.3 ADM (likely formal-only since ED is kinematic); Kretschmann and `R_{μν}R^{μν}` as quadratic-class close-out; dynamic-background extension for BEC-Extremal; update GR-SC 2.0 to include 1.7+1.8 when the five-class taxonomy stabilises.

- **2026-04-22 (eighth pass).** **Analytic derivation of ED-SC 2.0 `r* = −1.304` — four-memo arc, closed-form leading-order asymptotic achieved.** Following the sixth-pass flag ("analytical derivation of `r* = −1.304` from Scenario D structure"), a four-memo analytic chain now reaches from the Scenario-D PDE to a single-parameter transcendental equation for r*. **Four memos in ascending depth:** (1) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Derivation_Attempt.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Derivation_Attempt.md) — 3-parameter Gaussian+quadrupole ansatz; closed forms `T = −27π M_0/8` (trace invariant on pure-peak branch) and large-ε `r* = −5/27 ≈ −0.185`; target not reproduced; three obstructions identified (saddle vs peak, non-gradient M_2, filter conditioning). (2) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Derivation_Extended.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Derivation_Extended.md) — 4-mode Hermite–Gauss ansatz `δ = a_0ψ_00 + a_rρ²e^{−ρ²} + a_2ρ²cos(2θ)e^{−ρ²} + (c/2)ρ²sin(2θ)e^{−ρ²}`; identifies shape parameter `s = (a_r − a_0)/a_2` with `κ∥/κ⊥ = −(1+s)/(1−s)`; numerical saddle at `(β*, η*) ≈ (1.09, 0.48)` gives `s ≈ 0.13`, `κ∥/κ⊥ ≈ −1.3` (matches within 2%), but `λ_med/T ≈ +0.36` (sign mismatch — **indicates ED-SC 2.0 canonical r* is the spatial ratio κ∥/κ⊥, not the field-space ratio λ_med/Σλ**). (3) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Local_Geometry.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Local_Geometry.md) — works directly with the full 2D nonlinear saddle PDE and Freidlin–Wentzell quasi-potential; derives the variational obstruction `G[δ] = ½ M_2 δ |∇δ|²` (makes Ψ ≠ 2Φ); produces the headline symbolic formula `r* = 4μκ∥κ⊥ / [π + 2μ(κ∥²+κ⊥²) − M_2 δ_max(κ∥+κ⊥) − M_2 𝒦_NL]` with `μ = M(δ_max)`, `π = P'(δ_max)`; flags 𝒦_NL as the single nonlocal scalar correction. (4) [`theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Anisotropy.md`](../theory/ED_SC_2_0_r_star_Anisotropy.md) — Taylor-expands the saddle PDE to O(r²), derives the **anisotropy equation** `12μ(p−r) = (a−b)·[π − 6M_2 d(a+b)]` (new, local, relates quartic-asymmetry to quadratic-asymmetry); finds the **natural-amplitude closure** `δ_max² = −6P_0/P_3` at which the cubic nullcline forces the trace to vanish → **`s = κ∥/κ⊥ = −1` at leading order** (zero-trace saddle, PDE-level analytic, independent of M_0 and M_2); **produces the first closed-form asymptotic r* = −2χ/(2χ−1)** with `χ ≡ 2μκ⊥²/P_0`; matches target `r* = −1.304 ⟺ χ = 2.145 ⟺ κ⊥² ≈ 2.14` (physical O(1) motif width in natural units `M_0 = P_0 = |P_3| = 1`). **Durable structural findings (four that must remain stable in future sessions):** (a) **ED-SC 2.0's canonical `r* = −1.304` is the spatial principal-curvature ratio `κ∥/κ⊥`, not the field-space Hessian ratio `λ_med/Σλ`** — the Extended memo demonstrates these differ at O(1) and the field-space reading gives +0.36 at the best numerical saddle. Update ED-SC 2.0 §1.4 ambiguity (which "Hessian"): **spatial Hessian K of δ*** at the central stationary point, not field-space Hessian H of Ψ. (b) **The Scenario-D saddle sits exactly on the cubic nullcline** `δ_max² = −6P_0/P_3` at leading order; this is what makes the trace `κ∥+κ⊥ = 0` and therefore `s = −1`. The Extended memo's empirical `s ≈ −1.304` is a first-order shift `Δs = −0.304` encoded as `ε = (δ_max²/(−6P_0/P_3)) − 1` — a single scalar from the motif's anisotropic tail. (c) **The variational obstruction to ED being gradient flow is explicit and local:** drift differs from `−δΦ/δδ` by `G[δ] = ½ M_2 δ |∇δ|²`. Ψ = 2Φ + M_2 Ψ_1 + O(M_2²); Ψ_1 transport equation (3.9b of Local Geometry memo) is solvable along instantons from δ=0 to δ*. (d) **Three empirical scalars close the derivation end-to-end:** `κ⊥` (⊥-decay rate of the saddle), `ε` (amplitude shift from nullcline), `𝒦_NL` (M_2 nonlocal correction). All three are outputs of a single 2D elliptic solve of the Scenario-D PDE with motif-filter boundary data. **Boxed headline:** `r* = −2χ/(2χ−1)`, `χ = 2μκ⊥²/P_0`; full-order `r* = −2χ/[2χ − 1 − M_2 𝒦_NL/(2P_0)]`. **Durable memory:** [`memory/project_ed_r_star_analytic_arc.md`](../../.claude/projects/C--Users-allen-GitHub-Event-Density/memory/project_ed_r_star_analytic_arc.md) records the four memos + four durable findings + five guardrails for future sessions. **Next tangential theoretical targets (not yet executed):** numerical 2D elliptic solve of the saddle PDE to extract (κ⊥, ε, 𝒦_NL) at Scenario-D couplings; close the 𝒦_NL kernel (4.8 of Local Geometry) along the instanton; clarify ED-SC 2.0 §1.4 in the canonical doc (spatial vs field-space Hessian) so the definitional ambiguity cannot drift back.

- **2026-04-22 (seventh pass).** **External parallel work noted — Lohmiller & Slotine, "On computing quantum waves exactly from classical action," *Proc. R. Soc. A* 482 (2026) 20250413; arXiv:2405.06328.** SL construct Schrödinger wave functions exactly from a 𝕁-valued classical least-action field `φ_j(x, t)` plus classical density `ρ_j` transported along each extremal branch: `ψ_j = √ρ_j · exp(iφ_j/ℏ) · exp(−½ ∫₀ᵗ Δ_M φ_j dθ)`, `ψ = Σ_j ψ_j` (eq. 3.1). **Crucial technical point:** they retain the *pure classical* Hamilton-Jacobi p.d.e. — **no Bohm quantum potential `Q = −(ℏ²/2m)∇²√ρ/√ρ` is added**. "Quantum" behavior emerges entirely from (i) non-Lipschitz branch points where `Δ_M φ_j` is unbounded (generated by multiply-connected manifolds, inequality constraints, singularities, or multi-valued initial data), plus (ii) coherent summation across branches. Lemma 3.1 proves each `ψ_j` exactly solves Schrödinger (1.6); extends to Klein-Gordon / Pauli / Dirac / Maxwell; illustrated via double-slit, Aharonov-Bohm, particle-in-box, tunnelling, hydrogen, harmonic oscillator, EPR/spin. **Relation to ED (calibrated):** independent confirmation that `(density, action-like field)` is the right primitive pair for Schrödinger recovery — structurally parallel to ED's `(ρ, participation)` pairing in the reversible slice. **Significant differences:** SL is particle-mechanical on `ℝ^N` (not field-theoretic); SL's phase is the classical action satisfying HJ, while ED's participation is *not* an HJ action (relaxational ODE `τ ∂_t v = F[ρ] − ζ v`, part of a triad with saturation and dissipation); SL has no penalty, no mobility channel, no RG flow, no triad closure, no cross-scale invariance. SL claims *exact* Schrödinger/KG/Pauli/Dirac equivalence; ED claims only *reversible-slice consistency* with free scalar QFT (per `memory/project_ed10_geometry_qft_scope.md` guardrails). Both treat QM as *recovered*, not *axiomatic*. **Status:** calibrated citation added to [`theory/ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md §8`](../theory/ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md); SL should be cited as parallel external evidence for the density + action-like-field decomposition, **not** as evidence for any ED-specific claims (triad, RG closure, cross-scale invariance `r* = −1.304`, penalty saturation). **Speculative transferable tool** (flagged, not adopted): SL's branch-indexed mechanism — extremal action branches + `exp(−½ ∫ Δ_M φ dθ)` amplitude factor + coherent sum — could be examined for whether ED's participation field admits an analogous multi-branch construction along ED-SC 2.0's ray-extremal motifs. No ED doc or prediction changes on the strength of SL.

- **2026-04-22 (sixth pass).** **Wilsonian RG analysis of the canonical ED PDE completed — five memos closing the coarse-graining / flow-geometry / UV / IR / three-regime arc, plus the 0.6 problem resolution.** Math-only theoretical push following the ED-10 geometry closure. **Five durable structural results that must remain stable across future sessions:** (a) **ED operator basis is form-closed under Wilsonian coarse-graining.** At tree level and one loop, no operators outside `{M(ρ)∇²ρ + M'(ρ)|∇ρ|², P(ρ), τ v̇, ζ v, H v, D F[δ]}` are generated. The canonical ansatz is a theorem, not a guess. (b) **ED is NOT an RG fixed point at physical couplings.** At dynamic exponent `z = 2`: `β_{M_0} = 0` (marginal), `β_{P_0} = 2P_0`, `β_ζ = 2ζ`, `β_τ = −2τ`, `β_{P_3} = (2−2χ)P_3`, `β_{M_2} = −2χ M_2`. Non-trivial flow at any `P_0, ζ, τ ≠ 0`. (c) **Fixed-point catalog:** Gaussian `G = (M_0*, 0, 0, ∞)` (UV stable only), Wilson-Fisher fixed line at `χ = 1` (marginal cubic), nonlinear-mobility fixed line at `χ = 0` (marginal `M_2`), "fixed point at infinity" `(P_0 → ∞, ζ → ∞, τ → 0)` as IR sink; stability matrix is diagonal at all FPs. **Flow invariants** `P_0/ζ, P_0·τ, ζ·τ` are exactly RG-invariant. (d) **Two crossover scales bound the "ED window"** — `ℓ_v = ½ ln(ξ_v Λ)` (participation-slaving onset) and `ℓ_ξ = ln(ξ Λ)` (gap-dominated scale). ED-specific phenomenology (Q-C transition, C7 triad coupling, UDM β=2, saturating penalty) lives in `ℓ_v < ℓ < ℓ_ξ` only. (e) **Three-regime effective PDE structure, each regime boxed in the authoritative memos:** **UV** `∂_t δ = D M_0 ∇²δ + H v,  τ v̇ = M_0 ∇²δ` (free two-channel diffusion; v frozen at `τ → ∞`; wave-like dispersion — this is the kinematic acoustic-metric / free-scalar QFT regime from the fourth-pass arc). **Intermediate** `∂_t δ = Γ_eff [M_0 ∇²δ + (M_2/2) δ²∇²δ + M_2 δ|∇δ|² − P_0 δ − (P_3/6) δ³]` with `Γ_eff = D + H/ζ` (participation slaved, Model A universality). **IR** `∂_t δ = D M_0 ∇²δ − D P_0(ℓ) δ,  P_0(ℓ) → ∞` (linear gapped diffusion; δ → 0 exponentially; two-stage nonlinearity elimination). **Cross-scale invariance re-stated honestly:** the "ED across 20-60 OOM" claim is not coupling-invariance — couplings flow. It is **operator-structure invariance** within the intermediate window. Window location and coupling values are regime-specific. **The 0.6 problem closed in the same pass:** `0.6 = 2·D_nd(quantum)` as a structural dictionary identity, derived from `T_0 = L_0²·D_nd/D_phys` with `D_phys = ℏ/(2m)` (Madelung theorem) and `L_0 = ℏ/(mc)` (reduced Compton) → `T_0 = 2·D_nd·ℏ/(mc²) = 0.6·ℏ/(mc²)`. Five alternative routes audited (damping discriminant, reversible-slice QFT dispersion, acoustic-metric curvature, PME coarse-graining, ζ-interpolation) — all fail. The `c_0/c = 1/(2 D_nd)` side-identity gives `c_0 = c` exactly at `D_nd = 1/2`; current quantum-regime value `D_nd = 0.3` is the named structural feature. **Five authoritative memos (do not re-scope without reading these):** [`theory/The_0_6_Problem_Resolution.md`](../theory/The_0_6_Problem_Resolution.md), [`theory/ED_RG_Flow_Analysis.md`](../theory/ED_RG_Flow_Analysis.md), [`theory/ED_RG_Flow_Geometry.md`](../theory/ED_RG_Flow_Geometry.md), [`theory/ED_IR_Effective_PDE.md`](../theory/ED_IR_Effective_PDE.md), [`theory/ED_UV_PDE_and_Three_Regime_Flow.md`](../theory/ED_UV_PDE_and_Three_Regime_Flow.md). **Durable memory:** [`memory/project_ed_rg_three_regime.md`](../../.claude/projects/C--Users-allen-GitHub-Event-Density/memory/project_ed_rg_three_regime.md) records the nine structural results + seven guardrails for future sessions. **Guardrail summary:** ED is form-closed but not a fixed point; cross-scale invariance is structural in form not couplings; 0.6 is fixed by the dictionary, not free; IR slaving (v = F[δ]/ζ) vs UV freezing (v = v_0) are opposite limits of the same v-ODE; ED-specific phenomenology outside `[ℓ_v, ℓ_ξ]` is not supported by the effective PDE. **Tangential next theoretical targets (not yet executed):** analytical derivation of `r* = −1.304` from Scenario D structure (would upgrade cross-scale invariance from "structural form" to "specific number"), moving-background acoustic metric for the BEC extremal-horizon test, Noether / thermodynamic consistency on the intermediate PDE.

- **2026-04-22 (third pass).** **D_crit discrepancy resolved — Canon P6 single-number `D_crit = 0.5` retired in favour of the ζ-parametrised linearised form.** Full derivation in [`theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md`](../theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md). Linearising the canonical PDE around homogeneous equilibrium, Fourier-decomposing, and evaluating the 2×2 coupled-eigenvalue discriminant yields the underdamping condition `(D − ζ)² < 4(1 − D)` at reference mode `ε_k·τ = 1`, with critical threshold **`D_crit(ζ) = √(2−ζ)·(2 − √(2−ζ))`**. At canon-default `ζ = 1/4`, `D_crit ≈ 0.896`. At `ζ = 0`, `D_crit = 2√2 − 2 ≈ 0.828`. At `ζ → 1`, `D_crit → 1`. **The 00.2 Canon P6 heuristic `Δ = D + 2ζ, critical at Δ = 1 → D_crit = 1 − 2ζ = 0.5`** is not recoverable as any principled limit of the full discriminant (attempting to match via ε-rescaling yields the quadratic `4ε² − 36ε + 1 = 0` with roots ~8.97 and ~0.028, neither at the canonical `ε = 1`). **Root cause of the heuristic's ~80% error:** the additive form drops the coupled cross-term `(D − ζ)²` of the true discriminant, flips the sign of the cross-coupling (replacing `−2Dζ` with `+4Dζ`), and over-weights `ζ` by ~2×. **Ruled out as sources of the discrepancy:** dimensionality (per-mode eigenvalue problem is scalar in any `d`), mobility form (enters only via `M₀ = M(ρ*)` at linear order — β=1, β=2, SY2 all identical at linear order), penalty form (both linear and SY2 linearise to `P₀·δρ`), definitional ambiguity (both forms use `trace² = 4·det`). **Regime A (D=1, H=0, mobility-penalty only) has λ = −ε_k ∈ ℝ<0** — unconditionally overdamped, `D_crit` not defined in that regime. **Regime B (0<D<1) is where Canon P6 lives** and where the corrected formula applies. **Three verification hooks pass** (limits at ζ=0, ζ=1, monotonicity in ζ). §3 Canon P6 row and §4 three-regimes table updated. The "highest-priority v0.5+ theory issue" flagged 2026-04-20 in [`theory/ED-Dimensional-01-Ext.md`](../theory/ED-Dimensional-01-Ext.md) Appendix A is closed.

- **2026-04-20.** **AFM dewetting empirical track is now ED's highest-certainty near-term test.** ED-SC 2.0 §3 specifies a sharp falsification criterion for the motif-conditioned median of the field-space Hessian on 2D scalar density fields: `med(ℛ_motif(h(x,y))) ∈ [−1.50, −1.10]` for thin-film polymer dewetting in the spinodal pre-rupture regime. Standard AFM resolutions (50 nm lateral, 0.1 nm vertical) satisfy the §3 sampling requirement `Δx ≤ L_coh/8` by construction. **Pilot result (N=1, ℛ_all not ℛ_motif):** Scenario D simulation and one thin-film pilot frame agree at median = −2.063 vs −2.149, with overlapping IQRs ([−3.43, −1.49] vs [−3.96, −1.47]) and matching % in target band (21.7% vs 23.0%). The values fail the [−1.5, −1.1] band when read as ℛ_all, but the cross-system agreement is structurally suggestive that ℛ_all may carry architectural information beyond ED-SC 2.0's strict motif-conditioned claim. Real AFM data with `L_coh ≥ ~16 px` would unlock the motif filter. **Three routes to data, in increasing cost and certainty:** (1) browser-check 2023 *Nature Comm Phys* paper for accessible AFM data — 5 minutes; (2) email Jacobs group — second-cheapest, builds field connections; (3) book a 1–2 day session at any academic core facility with PS-on-Si dewetting samples — guaranteed canonical data by construction. **This is structurally separate from the ED-09.5 / Aspelmeyer / FRAP empirical track** — it tests ED-SC 2.0 (architectural invariants), not the Q-C transition. ED now has two independent empirical tracks running. **Operational recommendation:** execute Route 1 immediately; chain to 2/3 based on what Route 1 returns. AFM is the highest-certainty empirical path because it has a guaranteed-success physical-acquisition fallback (Route 3) that doesn't depend on any third party. New row added to §7 empirical-status table. **Route 3 is now operationalized** in [`AFM-Dewetting protocol`](../experiements/AFM-Dewetting-ED-SC_InProcess/protocol.md) — a session-ready canonical protocol (captured 2026-04-21) covering sample prep, scan parameters, data export, pre-analysis quality gates (including the pilot's root-cause fix: the `L_coh ≥ 8·Δx` sampling condition verified per-frame), ensemble statistics, and a five-outcome decision tree (PASS / NEAR-PASS / FAIL / UNDECIDABLE / SPLIT). ---

**Purpose.** This document captures ED framework content that lives **outside the repo** — in PhilArchive publications and in the user's local `Desktop/ED Interpretations/` and `Desktop/ED Important Papers/` folders — so that a new Claude Code session can acclimate in one read rather than rediscovering the scope from first principles. The repo is heavily focused on the PDE canon, UDM, merger-lag, and the dimensional atlas; the material below is *complementary* and sometimes *updates* what the repo says.

**The ED framework has three parallel tracks** that the repo does not make visible:

1. **The empirical physics program.** PDE canon → dimensional atlas → empirical tests in five regimes (quantum, Planck, condensed matter, galactic, cosmological). Concrete predictions, concrete falsification criteria. Lives mostly in the repo (UDM, Cluster Merger-Lag) and in 00.1 / 00.2 / 00.3 / ED-02 / ED-04 / ED-XX from the Desktop PDFs.
2. **The interpretive / ontological program.** Reframes existing phenomena in quantum mechanics, optics, information, topology, and spacetime itself as structural consequences of ED participation geometry. Produces structural *explanations*, not new measurements. Lives in ED-10 (spacetime emergence), the ED-I-XX interpretation series (photonics, quantum info, topology, weak lensing), and the PhilArchive philosophical papers (ED-06 / ED-07 / ED-08 / ED-09 / ED-09.5 / ED-13).
3. **The scale-correspondence program (ED-SC).** Identifies architectural invariants that recur across 20+ orders of magnitude. Treats micro ↔ macro correspondences as structural **identity**, not analogy. Lives in ED-SC-XX and the forthcoming scale-free atlas. First paper: ED-SC-00 (March 2026). See §6.6.

All three tracks share the same PDE canon and ontology (becoming, micro-events, participation, ED gradients). They differ in their goal: the empirical track tries to *predict* new measurements; the interpretive track tries to *unify* existing ones under one ontology; the scale-correspondence track tries to *identify architectural invariants* that persist when scale, mechanism, and substrate change.

**How to use this at session start.** Read §1 (scope & discrepancy map) first — it is the critical information. §3.1 (the two P1–P7 axiom sets — critical disambiguation) prevents confusing derivation axioms with the Canon. §5.9 (Architecture of Physical Law) is the **meta-claim** behind all three ED tracks: laws and symmetries are emergent, not fundamental. §6 (ED-XX environment sourcing revision) is the most important empirical-track update. §6.5 (Interpretation Series vocabulary) is the most important interpretive-track update. §11 (Emergence-Universe / ED-SIM sandbox) is the pre-ED proof-of-concept for the architecture-first thesis — disambiguate from the continuum `edsim/` solver. Skim §2–5 for depth. §7 is the empirical status snapshot. §8 is the full paper / code / GitHub map. §9 is the step-by-step checklist + question-type map. §12 is the non-physics Factor Skyline thread (kept for completeness, not session-start reading).

---

## 1. What the repo tells you vs. what the wider work says

### Things where the repo is authoritative and current

- The canonical PDE algebra (`theory/PDE.md`) — mobility, penalty, participation channels.
- UDM / mobility channel empirical fit (10 soft-matter materials, R² > 0.986).
- Cluster Merger-Lag evidence (7-cluster sample + Finner aggregate).
- Dimensional Atlas (5-regime mapping, D·T₀/L₀² = 0.3 invariant).
- Edsim simulation engine.
- Our work this session: RLC analogue memo, BTFR-Activity unified analysis, Finner-A1 test, scale-dependence scoping, etc.

### Things the repo does **not** currently contain (or contains in older form)

| Topic | Repo status | Wider-work status |
|---|---|---|

| **Channel-weight parameterization** | `D` is *dimensional diffusivity* (2.1×10²⁷ m²/s) in `theory/PDE.md` | Also `D` is *dimensionless channel weight* with `D+H=1` in [00.2, 00.3]. Two parameterizations of the same architecture — both valid at different abstraction layers. |

### Discrepancies you should know about at session start

1. **Penalty form.** The repo's `theory/PDE.md` uses the linear `P₀(ρ−ρ*)` form. The current canonical form per [00.3] is `P_SY2`. These agree near equilibrium but diverge at the mobility ceiling, and the horizon/heat-death arguments in [00.1] depend on SY2's saturation. If a future session touches `theory/PDE.md`, flag this before editing.
2. **What "D" means.** In repo code and repo docs, `D` is dimensional diffusivity (m²/s). In [00.2 Canon] and [00.3 Unified PDE], `D` is the dimensionless channel weight (with `D+H=1`). Context-sensitive.
3. **Galaxy-sourced vs. environment-sourced.** Any repo text or paper that asserts "galaxies generate their own temporal-tension halos" reflects the pre–April-2026 view. [ED-XX] supersedes this — galaxies set the *amplitude* via baryonic identity, the *spatial extent* comes from the cosmic web.

## 2. The trajectory (dated papers, in order)

The ED main series is numbered **ED-01 through ED-13** (with ED-04.5 and ED-09.5 as half-steps). The main series is complemented by the **00-series** (foundational cosmology math), the **ED-I series** (interpretive applications to quantum / optical / topological phenomena), the **ED-SC series** (scale-correspondence), the **ED-Arch / ED-Sim series** (architectural-invariants + Emergence-Universe sandbox; see §6.8 and §11), and the **ED-XX** revision. The Cluster Merger-Lag, Universal Degenerate-Mobility, and Open Note papers are empirical / methodological publications. The two **Factor Skyline** papers are a **separate non-physics thread** on multiplicative number theory (see §12 — kept in the inventory because Allen authors them, not because they are ED physics).

Not on Desktop under this name; accessible via PhilArchive. |

| **March 2026** | ED-SIM-3D | Canonical PDE 2D/3D Extension and Invariant Mini-Atlas | Dimensional-consistency validation. Extends the ED solver to d=1,2,3; runs 5 invariant tests (Barenblatt PME, RC decay, telegraph oscillation, horizon formation, participation coupling). Penalty + participation channels are dimension-independent to machine precision; mobility channel is dimension-dependent per `α_R = 1/(d(m-1)+2)`. Validates axiom P7. Runs on ED-SIM-02 software package. See §6.7. |
| **March 2026** | ED-Sim-01 / ED-Arch-01 | Architectural Invariants of Becoming: Experimental Probes | **First empirical validation of ED architectural invariants (v1.3).** Same paper filed under two series labels (Simulations + Architecture). 4×4 Scenario-D sweep on 512×512 lattice across mobility exponent `n ∈ {0.5, 1, 2, 4}` and Langevin noise `σ ∈ {0.01, 0.02, 0.05, 0.10}`. Finds a saddle-shaped phase-exit surface with peak at `(n=2.7, σ=0.0556)`, step 457. Curvature ratio κ_∥/κ_⊥ ≈ −1.3 ± 0.2 matches the Local Group mass sheet and Casimir cavity. Four regimes empirically identified. **Does NOT contain the 1/r dilution argument.** See §6.8. |
| **March 2026** | ED-Arch-02 | Architectural Foundations of Event Density | Theoretical counterpart to ED-Arch-01. Defines saddle / channel / boundary / horizon via Hessian geometry (gradient sign-flip, det(H)=0 curves, λ_⊥ > 0 for boundaries, λ_⊥ < 0 for horizons). Derives universality (IC-independence, parameter-deformation stability, noise-threshold robustness, mobility-law invariance, curvature-driven necessity). See §6.8. |
| **April 2026** | ED-XX | Environment Sourcing of Temporal Tension | Major revision. Galaxy-sourced hypothesis overturned by a 3D Green's-function `1/r` dilution argument. **Source document NOT located** — it is NOT ED-SIM-3D, NOT ED-Sim-01 / ED-Arch-01, NOT ED-Arch-02. Likely lives inside the ED-XX paper itself. |
| (in repo) | Cluster Merger-Lag | Cluster Merger-Lag Evidence | 7-cluster sample + Finner aggregate test `ℓ = D_T/v_current`. Currently the primary-cited empirical penalty-channel test. |

**Separate thread — not part of the ED physics program:** Regulated Multiplicity: An Architectural Account of Consciousness (Dec 2025) and Regulated Multiplicity: An AI Systems Architecture (Jan 2026). Confirmed independently as philosophy-of-mind / AI systems work with no physics content.

## 3. The Architectural Canon (7 principles) — P1 through P7

From [00.2 March 2026]. Any PDE satisfying these is "architecturally ED," regardless of functional form.

| # | Principle | Statement |
|---|---|---|
| **P1** | Operator Structure | `F[ρ] = M(ρ)∇²ρ + M'(ρ)\|∇ρ\|² − P(ρ)` — curvature-dependent diffusion + nonlinear gradient + restoring force |
| **P2** | Channel Complementarity | `ρ̇ = D·F[ρ] + H·v`, `D + H = 1`, `D,H ∈ [0,1]` — direct + mediated channels, convex weighting |
| **P3** | Penalty Equilibrium | `P(ρ*) = 0` with `P' > 0` — unique globally-attracting equilibrium |
| **P4** | Mobility Capacity Bound | `M(ρ_max) = 0` with `M(ρ) > 0` for `ρ < ρ_max` — horizon at the capacity bound |
| **P5** | Participation Feedback Loop | `v̇ = (1/τ)(F[ρ] − ζv)` — memory channel with exponential decay |
| **P6** | Damping Discriminant | **Linearised form (resolved 2026-04-22, [`theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md`](../theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md)):** underdamped iff `(D − ζ)² < 4(1 − D)` at reference mode `ε_k·τ = 1`; critical threshold `D_crit(ζ) = √(2−ζ)·(2 − √(2−ζ))`; at canon-default `ζ = 1/4`, **`D_crit ≈ 0.896`** (NOT 0.5). The earlier additive heuristic `Δ = D + 2ζ, critical at Δ = 1 → D_crit = 0.5` is retired as quantitative claim (error ~80%); retained only as order-of-magnitude mnemonic. |
| **P7** | Nonlinear Triad Coupling | `M'(ρ)·\|∇ρ\|²` generates k=3 from k=1 with invariant triad ratio. **Calibrated 2026-04-22** — scale-free invariant `K = A₃/A₁³ ≈ 0.0148 ± 0.0005`, companion `K₂ = A₂/A₁² ≈ 0.279`, cubic scaling slope `α₃ = 3.0 ± 0.05`, exact phase lock `φ₃ − 3φ₁ = π` (SD ~ 10⁻⁶ rad), symmetry ordering `A₂ > A₃` in the clean regime (~200× at A₁=0.1 per simulation). The amplitude-dependent ratio `A₃/A₁` is NOT the invariant; the previously-cited ED-Phys-16 "3–6%" band reproduces only in the saturation regime at `A₁ ≳ 0.15·ρ_max`. Operational test: [`experiements/Triad-Coupling-C7_InProcess/protocol.md`](../experiements/Triad-Coupling-C7_InProcess/protocol.md). |

Counterfactual analysis: removing any principle breaks a specific architectural layer (motifs / laws / geometry / invariants). The Canon is minimal and irreducible.

**Why this matters for me:** when I read repo docs that refer to "the ED PDE," I now know this is shorthand for the equivalence class defined by P1–P7. The specific mobility and penalty forms in `theory/PDE.md` are one instance. The RLC-analogue memo I wrote derives P6 (damping discriminant) in dimensional units without knowing it was P6 — worth cross-linking if I revisit it. **P7 addendum (2026-04-22):** the Triad-Coupling-C7 simulation companion at [`analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md`](../analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md) reduced P7 from a qualitative "k=3-from-k=1" claim to a sharp four-observable invariant (`K, K₂, α₃, Δφ`). The historical `A₃/A₁ ∈ [0.02, 0.08]` band inherited from ED-Phys-16 is retired as a primary criterion; `K = A₃/A₁³` is the replacement scale-free invariant. The "A₂ < A₃ by odd symmetry" claim in earlier drafts of the C7 protocol was **inverted** — the quadratic `M′(ρ)|∇ρ|²` sources the second harmonic directly via the DC + 2k structure of `|∇ρ|²`, so `A₂ > A₃` in the clean regime.

### 3.1 The two P1–P7 axiom sets — critical disambiguation

**There are TWO distinct "P1–P7" axiom sets in the ED corpus, used at different layers of the theory.** Prior Claude sessions have conflated them. When reading any ED document that references "P1" through "P7," first determine which set is being invoked:

| Set | Source | Purpose | Symbol for what's constrained |
|:---|:---|:---|:---|
| **Derivation axioms** | `ED_Foundational_Paper(.md / v2.md)` §2.4, `ED-Math-01_Uniqueness_Well-Posedness_and_Architectural_Laws.md` Theorem 2.1, `WHAT_IS_ED.md` | Axioms from which the canonical PDE is **derived**. These determine *what the PDE must look like*. Theorem 2.1 proves the canonical ED PDE is the unique second-order scalar PDE satisfying all seven. | P1 = Locality · P2 = Isotropy · P3 = Gradient-driven flow · P4 = Dissipative structure · P5 = Single scalar field · P6 = Minimal coupling · P7 = Dimensional consistency |
| **Architectural Canon (00.2)** | `00.2 Architectural Canon of the Unified ED Cosmology PDE`, `Desktop/ED Important Papers/The Architectural Canon...pdf` | Principles defining ED as a **class** of PDEs. These specify *what structural features every architecturally-ED PDE must have*. Any PDE satisfying these is "architecturally ED," regardless of specific functional forms. | P1 = Operator Structure · P2 = Channel Complementarity (D+H=1) · P3 = Penalty Equilibrium · P4 = Mobility Capacity Bound · P5 = Participation Feedback Loop · P6 = Damping Discriminant (D_crit = 0.5) · P7 = Nonlinear Triad Coupling |

**They are complementary, not contradictory.** The derivation axioms operate at the level of PDE *form* (what mathematical objects are allowed to appear); the Canon principles operate at the level of PDE *architecture* (what structural relations must hold among those objects). A PDE satisfying only the derivation axioms might not be "architecturally ED" unless it also satisfies the Canon; a PDE satisfying the Canon principles has, by construction, the canonical form the derivation axioms produce.

**The ED-13 "seven axioms" claim** ("four primitives and seven axioms uniquely determine the equation") most naturally refers to the **derivation-axiom set** (ED-Math-01 Theorem 2.1), composed with the four ED-05 pre-PDE axioms (non-negativity, null baseline, monotonicity, subadditivity). The 00.2 Canon is a *structural characterization* of what the derivation yields, not an independent set of axioms layered on top.

**When an ED paper says "P4":**
- If the paper is the Foundational Paper, ED-Math-01, or any uniqueness-theorem context → P4 = Dissipative structure.
- If the paper is 00.2, 00.3, any "Canon" context, or any paper citing `D_crit = 0.5` → P4 = Mobility Capacity Bound.
- **If in doubt, check which set of seven labels appears nearby.** The two sets have no overlapping labels.

The three-track structure documented at the top of this doc (Empirical / Interpretive / Scale-correspondence) generally uses whichever axiom set is most convenient for the current abstraction layer. Both sets are correct; neither is deprecated.

### 3.2 Axioms stack: four ED-05 → seven derivation → seven Canon

For session-start reference, the full axiom stack from pre-PDE to architectural:

1. **Pre-PDE layer (ED-05, Feb 2026, 4 axioms on a bare event domain):** non-negativity, null baseline, monotonicity, subadditivity. No time, geometry, or probability presupposed.
2. **Derivation layer (Foundational Paper / ED-Math-01, 7 axioms):** locality, isotropy, gradient-driven flow, dissipative structure, single scalar field, minimal coupling, dimensional consistency. ED-Math-01 Theorem 2.1: these **uniquely determine** the canonical PDE up to the choice of constitutive functions `M(ρ)` and `P(ρ)`.
3. **Architectural Canon layer (00.2, 7 principles):** operator structure, channel complementarity, penalty equilibrium, mobility capacity bound, participation feedback loop, damping discriminant, nonlinear triad coupling. Specifies the structural *architecture* the derived PDE must exhibit.

A PDE that passes all 4+7+7 is guaranteed to reproduce the ED phenomenology: unique attractor, Lyapunov dissipation, three-stage convergence, oscillation-death at D_crit = 0.5, and the 22-correspondence scale-invariance of ED-SC Table 1.

---

## 4. The Unified Cosmological Equation (00.3 canon)

The canonical PDE in its current cleanest form:

$$\partial_t \rho = D \cdot F[\rho] + H \cdot v, \qquad D + H = 1$$
$$\partial_t v = \frac{1}{\tau}(F[\rho] - \zeta v)$$
$$F[\rho] = M(\rho)\nabla^2\rho + M'(\rho)|\nabla\rho|^2 - P_{SY2}(\rho)$$
$$P_{SY2}(\rho) = \alpha\gamma \cdot \frac{\rho - \rho^*}{\sqrt{(\rho-\rho^*)^2 + \rho_0^2}}$$

### Three regimes (parameter-determined)

| Regime | Condition (heuristic boundaries, 00.3) | Corrected boundary (2026-04-22) | Behavior |
|---|---|---|---|
| Oscillatory | `D < 0.1` | `D ≪ D_crit(ζ)` — well below threshold | Underdamped, reversible, standing participation waves, 8–19 transient oscillations |
| Transitional / Hybrid | `0.1 ≤ D ≤ 0.4` | `D → D_crit(ζ)` from below | Mixed behavior, smooth interpolation |
| Parabolic | `D ≥ 0.5` | `D ≥ D_crit(ζ) ≈ 0.896` at canon-default `ζ = 1/4` | Overdamped, irreversible, structure-forming, peak merging, basin formation |

**Note (2026-04-22):** The original heuristic boundaries (`< 0.1`, `0.1–0.4`, `≥ 0.5`) were calibrated against the retired `D_crit = 0.5` heuristic. Full linearised analysis places the parabolic/hybrid boundary at `D_crit(ζ) ≈ 0.9` (canon-default). The qualitative three-regime structure survives; the numerical boundaries shift upward by ~0.4 in D. Downstream papers (ED-SIM-3D §6.7, Extended Atlas §5–§7) that used the 0.5 threshold as a regime marker should be re-examined. See [`theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md`](../theory/D_crit_Resolution_Memo.md) §10.

### Universal invariants

- **Equilibrium density** `ρ*` — unique zero of P_SY2, globally attracting across all D ∈ [0,1].
- **Ground state energy** `E_ground = αγρ₀` — independent of dimension, mixing ratio, IC.
- **Relaxation timescale** `t_rel ≈ ρ₀/(αγ)` — varies only ~13% across the entire hybrid parameter space.
- **Horizon behavior** — near `ρ_max`, mobility collapses (diffusion vanishes), but participation v and its inertia survive. This produces oscillating horizons in the oscillatory regime (lifetime extended by ~60%) and collapsing horizons in the parabolic regime.

### Nonlinear structure (weakly coupled)

- Triad resonance `k_3 = k_1 ± k_2`, coupling **~0.03 (provenance unclear; ED-Phys-16 fit at undocumented N)**. See [`analysis/ED_SC_2_0_Sample_Size_Audit.md`](../analysis/ED_SC_2_0_Sample_Size_Audit.md) §2.2. The C7 deterministic-canonical-operator result ([`analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md`](../analysis/scripts/telegraph_pme/triad_calibration/memo.md)) gives `K = A₃/A₁³ = 0.0148 ± 0.0005` on a fixed monochromatic IC; whether K and the "0.03" refer to the same object is an open provenance question.
- Harmonic generation at **3–6% of fundamental (provenance unclear; requires citation or re-run)**. The C7-derived form `A₃/A₁ = K·A₁²` with K = 0.0148 gives 3% at A₁ ≈ 1.4 and is the preferred successor statement.
- No mode locking, no chaos, no bifurcations.
- ED is "a weakly nonlinear, weakly coupled, nearly non-dispersive oscillator lattice with reversible participation dynamics."

## 5. The ontology (ED-10 emergence map)

Becoming is primitive. Micro-events are atomic units. Participation is the relational substrate. Everything geometric / informational / temporal is emergent.

### Coarse-graining dictionary

| Classical concept | ED substrate |
|---|---|
| Space | stable participation adjacency |
| Time | commitment order (irreversible) |
| Distance | participation resistance |
| Curvature | ED gradient structure |
| Locality | thick participation coherence |
| Mass / energy | patterns of committed micro-events |
| Horizons | decoupling surfaces / participation bottlenecks |
| Einstein's equations | **not** emergent from ED. Only a kinematic acoustic metric `g^eff_μν = diag(−M(ρ_0), 1, 1, 1)` arises (ii-grade, slaved to `ρ_0`, no field equation). Schwarzschild unreachable under any coordinate transformation. See [`ED_Effective_Acoustic_Metric.md`](../theory/ED_Effective_Acoustic_Metric.md) + [`ED_Schwarzschild_Obstruction.md`](../theory/ED_Schwarzschild_Obstruction.md). |
| Schrödinger evolution | **not** derived from ED. In the reversible slice (`D = 0, ζ = 0`), linearised ED is a free massive Klein-Gordon field whose canonical quantisation is consistent with Schrödinger-picture free-scalar QFT — a consistency result, not a derivation of QM. See [`ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md`](../theory/ED_Reversible_Sector_QFT.md). |
| Wavefunction collapse | irreversible selection of a participation channel |
| Born rule | participation weights |
| Entanglement | shared uncommitted participation structure |
| Information | constraint on viable commitment histories |
| Holography | constraint imposed by decoupling surfaces |
| Entropy | distribution of viable commitment histories |
| Arrow of time | asymmetry of commitment (ontological, not statistical) |

### Continuum

Quantum → Relational → Classical → Geometric. One substrate (participation), regime-dependent expressions.

**Note on scope.** ED-10 is philosophical/architectural, not empirically discriminating. The empirical program lives in the mobility / penalty / participation tests. ED-10 is what makes the framework a *unifying ontology* rather than just a DM alternative, but claims like "the measurement problem dissolves" are interpretive, not tested.
